# ============================================================================
# CHAOS REDUX - EVENT 005 SOVIET COLLAPSE TRIGGERS
# ============================================================================
# Shared readable triggers for the Soviet Collapse crisis, breakaway countries,
# Soviet mission board, and foreign intervention layer.
# ============================================================================

is_soviet_collapse_active = {
	has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_active
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_resolved_by_reconquest }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
}

is_soviet_collapse_aftermath_active = {
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_resolved_by_reconquest }
	OR = {
		is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
		has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_recovered_original_union_territory = {
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_original_union_territory_marked
	all_state = {
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_state_flag = soviet_collapse_original_union_state }
			is_controlled_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_enter_calm_strong_center_state = {
	has_soviet_collapse_strong_center_facts = yes
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_republic_confidence_cap compare = less_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_depot_vulnerability_cap compare = less_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_foreign_appetite_cap compare = less_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_league_cohesion_cap compare = less_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_old_movement_cap compare = less_than_or_equals }
}

has_soviet_collapse_strong_center_facts = {
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
	NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.strong_center_authority_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.strong_center_obedience_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 } }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
}

must_soviet_collapse_exit_calm_strong_center_state = {
	OR = {
		has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse
		has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.strong_center_authority_exit_gate compare = less_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.strong_center_obedience_exit_gate compare = less_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_republic_confidence_cap compare = greater_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_depot_vulnerability_cap compare = greater_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_foreign_appetite_cap compare = greater_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_league_cohesion_cap compare = greater_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_old_movement_cap compare = greater_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_complete_objective_now = {
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_objective_activation_grace }
}

can_soviet_collapse_activate_opening_followup_objectives = {
	OR = {
		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_objective_staging }
		AND = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes }
		}
		has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = {
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_state
	NOT = { must_soviet_collapse_exit_calm_strong_center_state = yes }
}

is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = {
	has_soviet_collapse_strong_center_facts = yes
	check_variable = {
		var = soviet_collapse_months_active
		value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_strong_center_guard_months
		compare = less_than
	}
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_last_month_total_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
}

has_soviet_collapse_baltic_breakaway = {
	OR = {
		LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_anti_soviet_breakaway_war = {
	OR = {
		UKR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		BLR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		MOL = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		GEO = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		ARM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		AZR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		UZB = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		KYR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		TAJ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		TMS = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		KAZ = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		KAR = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		KOM = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		CRI = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		TAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		BSK = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		FER = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		SMI = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		FEV = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor has_war_with = SOV }
		SZA = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor has_war_with = SOV }
		UWD = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor has_war_with = SOV }
		MRC = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor has_war_with = SOV }
		YAK = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		BYA = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
		TAN = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway has_war_with = SOV }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_visible_war_release_pressure = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.low_threat
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.war_release_breakaway_gate
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_obedience
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_major_war_release_pressure = {
	has_war_with_major = yes
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_obedience
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = {
	OR = {
		NOT = { capital_scope = { is_controlled_by = ROOT } }
		has_soviet_collapse_major_war_release_pressure = yes
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_anti_soviet_breakaway_war = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_visible_war_release_pressure = yes
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.republic_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.foreign_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.high_threat
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = {
	OR = {
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_failure_release_pressure = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_severe_component_release_pressure = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.high_threat
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.real_release_pressure_urgency_gate
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.critical_authority
			compare = less_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_obedience
			compare = less_than
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_component_release_pressure = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_pressure_high
			compare = greater_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_pressure_high
			compare = greater_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_pressure_high
			compare = greater_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_pressure_high
			compare = greater_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_old_movement_pressure_high
			compare = greater_than
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.republic_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.depot_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.foreign_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.league_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.old_movement_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_severe_component_release_pressure = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_republic_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_depot_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_foreign_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_league_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_old_movement_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_strategic_release_failure = {
	OR = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_union_archives_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_loyal_military_districts_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_tashkent_anchor_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_mountain_administration_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_factory_gates_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_basmachi_supply_chain_failed
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_protected_strong_center_release_window = {
	OR = {
		is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
		is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_strong_center_facts = yes
	}
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat compare = less_than }
	NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes }
	NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes }
	NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
	NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
}

is_soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention_pressure_open = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	has_soviet_collapse_foreign_specific_intervention_pressure = yes
	OR = {
		NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_protected_strong_center_release_window = yes }
		has_soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention_real_pressure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_foreign_specific_intervention_pressure = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
	OR = {
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.latent_foreign_pressure_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.moscow_authority
					compare = less_than
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_baseline.military_obedience
					compare = less_than
				}
				has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
				has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
			}
		}
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.intervention_catalyst_foreign_appetite_gate
				compare = greater_than
			}
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
				has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention_real_pressure = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
	has_soviet_collapse_foreign_specific_intervention_pressure = yes
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.foreign_pressure
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.intervention_catalyst_foreign_appetite_gate
				compare = greater_than
			}
			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
				has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_accept_foreign_patron_pressure = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	OR = {
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
		has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock
			has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_opening_pressure_initialized
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_lock_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = less_than }
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				is_soviet_collapse_calm_strong_center_window = yes
				is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_strong_center_facts = yes
			}
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = less_than }
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_authority compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.contested_component_cap_breakaway_gate compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.moderate_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 } }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.severe_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_terminal_collapse }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_terminal_pacing_matured = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_foreign_patron_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.preterminal_foreign_patron_month_cap compare = less_than }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 } }
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_failure_release_pressure = {
	OR = {
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_strategic_release_failure = yes
			OR = {
				NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_early_failure_release_guard_window = yes }
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_months_active
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_strong_center_guard_months
						compare = less_than
					}
					has_soviet_collapse_opening_failure_release_count = yes
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = soviet_collapse_months_active
							value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_strong_center_guard_months
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					has_soviet_collapse_early_failure_release_count = yes
				}
				has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
				has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
			}
		}
		AND = {
			is_soviet_collapse_early_failure_release_guard_window = yes
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						var = soviet_collapse_months_active
						value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_strong_center_guard_months
						compare = less_than
					}
					has_soviet_collapse_opening_failure_release_count = yes
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							var = soviet_collapse_months_active
							value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.opening_strong_center_guard_months
							compare = less_than
						}
					}
					has_soviet_collapse_early_failure_release_count = yes
				}
			}
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_early_failure_release_guard_window = yes }
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
				check_variable = {
					var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives
					value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_mountain_administration_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_ural_factory_gates_failed
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_basmachi_supply_chain_failed
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_fire_progressive_release_report = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_roll_confirmed
	has_event_target = soviet_collapse_release_target
}

has_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pacing_ready = {
	OR = {
		AND = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_opening_strong_center_guard_window = yes }
			NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_calm_mtth_release_block = yes }
		}
		AND = {
				NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_union_unmade_first_month_lock }
				NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_calm_mtth_release_block = yes }
				OR = {
					has_soviet_collapse_neighbor_mtth_release_pressure = yes
					has_soviet_collapse_post_opening_breakaway_mtth_pressure = yes
					has_soviet_collapse_low_threat_follow_on_release_lane = yes
					has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
					has_soviet_collapse_failure_release_pressure = yes
					has_soviet_collapse_release_level_component_pressure = yes
			}
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency = yes
			has_soviet_collapse_opening_release_emergency_severity = yes
		}
		has_soviet_collapse_low_threat_follow_on_release_lane = yes
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_accelerated_terminal_severity = {
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
			compare = greater_than
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.min_breakaways_for_union_unmade
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_critical_authority
			compare = less_than
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.critical_obedience
				compare = less_than
			}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_last_month_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_accelerated_failure_gate
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_accelerated_failure_gate
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		has_soviet_collapse_severe_component_release_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_real_regional_cascade_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_strategic_release_failure = yes
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
	}
}

				value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.deep_collapse_threat
				compare = greater_than

		AND = {

				var = soviet_collapse_months_active
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_catastrophic_active_months
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat
				compare = greater_than

				compare = less_than

		AND = {

				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_accelerated_active_months
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months

				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}

			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_war_release_pressure = yes
				has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_announced
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_kazakhstan_first_wave_failed
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_months_active
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_active_months
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_terminal_pressure_months
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_terminal_pressure_months
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_accumulated_release_pressure = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	NOT = { has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_cooldown }
	OR = {
		NOT = { has_soviet_collapse_calm_mtth_release_block = yes }
		has_soviet_collapse_low_threat_follow_on_release_lane = yes
	}
	has_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pacing_ready = yes
	OR = {
		has_soviet_collapse_real_release_pressure = yes
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_latent_mtth_release_pressure = yes
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_mature_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_neighbor_mtth_release_pressure = yes
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_roll_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_post_opening_breakaway_mtth_pressure = yes
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_roll_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_low_threat_follow_on_roll_ready = yes
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_compound_latent_mtth_release_pressure = yes
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.compound_latent_pressure_roll_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_failed_months
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.failed_month_roll_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_roll_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}
	has_soviet_collapse_sustained_mtth_release_pressure = yes
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate_count value = 0 compare = greater_than }
	OR = {
		check_variable = {
			var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
			value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_roll_gate
			compare = greater_than_or_equals
		}
		AND = {
			has_soviet_collapse_low_threat_follow_on_roll_ready = yes
		}
		AND = {
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_release_urgency_score
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.real_release_pressure_urgency_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
			check_variable = {
				var = soviet_collapse_progressive_release_pressure
				value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_mtth.sustained_pressure_miss_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_progressive_release_candidate = {
	OR = {
		tag = UKR

		tag = TMS

			OR = {
				has_soviet_collapse_two_smaller_central_asian_republics_free = yes
				AND = {
					is_soviet_collapse_southern_breakaway_active = yes
					SOV = {
						OR = {
							check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_obedience compare = less_than }
							check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.foreign_pressure compare = greater_than_or_equals }
							check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.old_movement_pressure compare = greater_than_or_equals }
						}
					}
				}
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		AND = {
			OR = {
				tag = KAR
				tag = KOM
				tag = CRI
				tag = TAT
				tag = BSK
				tag = FER
				tag = YAK
				tag = BYA
				tag = TAN
				tag = SMI
			}
				OR = {
					SOV = {
						check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.moderate_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
					has_global_flag = soviet_collapse_evolution_first_wave_recorded
					SOV = {
						check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.early_breakaway_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
					}
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 3 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
				has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
			}
		}
		is_soviet_collapse_dynamic_union_progressive_release_candidate = yes
	}
	NOT = { is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_first_wave_republics value = THIS } }
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_moscow_federated_subject }
	OR = {
		AND = {
			exists = no
			any_state = {
					is_core_of = PREV
					OR = {
						is_owned_by = SOV
						is_controlled_by = SOV
					owner = { is_subject_of = SOV }
					controller = { is_subject_of = SOV }
					owner = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
					controller = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
					owner = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
					controller = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic }
					owner = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor }
					controller = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor }
				}
			}
		}
		AND = {
			exists = yes
			is_subject_of = SOV
		}
	}
}

		num_of_military_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_military_factories
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_divisions

		is_major = yes

		SOV = {

				value = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.intervention_catalyst_foreign_appetite_gate
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
	}

		num_of_military_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_military_factories
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_divisions
		AND = {
			is_major = yes
			NOT = { has_government = democratic }
		}
	}
}

	OR = {
		AND = {
			exists = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
				}
				OR = {
					is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
				}
			NOT = { tag = SOV }
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = {
			exists = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
				}
				OR = {
					is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
				}
			NOT = { tag = SOV }
			NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
		}
	}
	NOT = { tag = SOV }
}

				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
				is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
			}
			NOT = { tag = SOV }
		}
		AND = {
			FROM = {
				exists = yes
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
				}
				OR = {
					is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					is_in_array = { array = global.soviet_collapse_breakaway_countries value = THIS }
				}
				NOT = { tag = SOV }
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
					NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_recent }
				}
			}
			NOT = { tag = SOV }
			OR = {
				FROM = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_sponsor_recent }
			}

		}
	}

				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member
			}

		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_sponsor_recent }

		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_major_aid_sponsor_recent }

	}

			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_member
		}
	}
	OR = {

		is_soviet_collapse_league_conference_patron_style = yes
		is_soviet_collapse_relief_patron_style = yes
		is_soviet_collapse_reconstruction_patron_style = yes
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_target_acceptance_for_foreign_aid_from_root = {
	FROM = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SOV
			NOT = { has_stability > constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.target_stability_ceiling }
			NOT = { has_war_support > constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.target_war_support_ceiling }
			NOT = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.target_acceptance_equipment_floor } }
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_corridor_open
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_recognition_progress value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.target_acceptance_recognition_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.target_acceptance_resilience_need_ceiling compare = less_than }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.target_acceptance_patronage_ceiling compare = less_than }
		}
	}
	NOT = {
		AND = {
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_dominant_sponsor_lock
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.target_acceptance_patronage_ceiling compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three }
			}
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_relief_patron_style = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_league_conference_patron_style = yes }
		}
	}
	OR = {
		FROM = { NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_republic_protected_from_external_dependency = yes } }
		FROM = { has_war_with = SOV }
		FROM = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_corridor_open }
		is_soviet_collapse_relief_patron_style = yes
		is_soviet_collapse_league_conference_patron_style = yes
	}
	NOT = {
		AND = {
			is_soviet_collapse_client_patron_style = yes
			FROM = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk value = constant:soviet_collapse_influence_war.stage_2_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_two }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_balanced_sponsors_three }
			}
		}
	}
}

	OR = {

			is_soviet_collapse_league_conference_patron_style = yes

has_soviet_collapse_major_foreign_aid_route_to_from = {
	OR = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
		FROM = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target }
		FROM = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_corridor_open }
		has_soviet_collapse_direct_foreign_aid_border_to_from = yes
		AND = {
			any_controlled_state = { is_coastal = yes }
			FROM = { any_controlled_state = { is_coastal = yes } }
		}
	}

	any_controlled_state = {
		any_neighbor_state = {
			is_controlled_by = FROM
		}
	}

			FROM = { any_controlled_state = { is_coastal = yes } }
		}

is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = {
	OR = {
		is_major = yes
		num_of_civilian_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_civilian_factories
		num_of_military_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_military_factories
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_divisions
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_free_republics_league_founder
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength value = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_institution_strength compare = greater_than_or_equals }
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_regional_target = {
	NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes }
	OR = {
		is_in_faction = yes
		num_of_civilian_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_civilian_factories
		num_of_military_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_military_factories
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_divisions
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_recognition_progress value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.large_recognition_gain compare = greater_than }
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_strong_foreign_dependency_target = {
	OR = {
		is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.strong_republic_divisions
		num_of_civilian_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_civilian_factories
		num_of_military_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_military_factories
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength value = constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.priority_target_institution_strength compare = greater_than_or_equals }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_dynamic_foreign_dependency_resilience_room = {
	OR = {
		AND = {
			is_soviet_collapse_strong_foreign_dependency_target = yes
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience value = constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.strong_republic_resilience_ceiling compare = less_than }
		}
		AND = {
			is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_strong_foreign_dependency_target = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience value = constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.major_target_resilience_ceiling compare = less_than }
		}
		AND = {
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_major_target = yes }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_strong_foreign_dependency_target = yes }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience value = constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.target_resilience_ceiling compare = less_than }
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_dynamic_foreign_dependency_influence_ready_for_from = {
	OR = {
		FROM = { NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_strong_foreign_dependency_target = yes } }
		FROM = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_total value = constant:soviet_collapse_puppet_pressure.strong_republic_total_influence_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_launch_high_chaos_offensive = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
	SOV = { exists = yes is_soviet_collapse_active = yes }
	NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
	can_declare_war_on = SOV
	can_pay_soviet_collapse_breakaway_high_chaos_offensive_cost = yes
	OR = {
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 4 }
		has_global_flag = { flag = chaos_tier value = 5 }
		SOV = { check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_super_event.union_unmade_high_threat compare = greater_than } }
	}
	OR = {
		num_divisions > constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_action.offensive_min_divisions
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_institution_strength value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.medium_recognition_gain compare = greater_than }
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_field_emergency_battalions_raised
	}
}

can_target_soviet_collapse_regional_security_zone_mandate = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_leader = yes
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_league_external_mandates_unlocked
	FROM = {
		exists = yes
		is_neighbor_of = ROOT
		NOT = { tag = ROOT }
		NOT = { tag = SOV }
		NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
		NOT = { is_in_faction_with = ROOT }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor }
		OR = {
			is_major = yes
			any_controlled_state = { is_coastal = yes }
			num_of_civilian_factories > constant:soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention.regional_target_civilian_factories
		}
	}
	can_declare_war_on = FROM
	NOT = { has_wargoal_against = FROM }
}

is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_candidate = {
	is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
	OR = {
		is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
	}
	OR = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
	}
	NOT = { tag = SOV }
	NOT = { is_subject = yes }
	NOT = { is_in_faction = yes }
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction }
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recently_left }
}

has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_member_ready = {
	OR = {
		LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_baltic_league_quorum = {
	OR = {
		AND = {
			LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
			LAT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		AND = {
			LIT = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
			EST = { exists = yes has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway }
		}
		AND = {

is_soviet_collapse_regional_league_foundation_pressure_ready = {
	OR = {
		is_soviet_collapse_league_pressure_ready = yes
		SOV = {
			exists = yes
			OR = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_breakaway_count value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.one_breakaway_count compare = greater_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.high_foreign_appetite_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_monthly_failed_objectives value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.failure_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
		}
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_leader = {
	has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction
	is_faction_leader = yes
}

has_active_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal = {
	OR = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_defense_goal
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recognition_goal
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_logistics_goal
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_success = {
	is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_leader = yes
	has_active_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal = yes
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_recently_resolved }
	OR = {
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_defense_goal
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_league_defensive_war_called
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recognition_goal
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_recognition_progress value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_success_recognition compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_logistics_goal
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_control value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_success_depot compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		}
	}
}

has_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_failure = {
	is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_leader = yes
	has_active_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal = yes
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_goal_recently_resolved }
	OR = {
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_tension value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_failure_tension_threshold compare = greater_than_or_equals }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.goal_failure_cohesion_floor compare = less_than }
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_defense_goal
			SOV = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_threat_guard.calm_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
			}
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
		}
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_recognition_goal
			SOV = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_breakaway_support.high_foreign_appetite_gate compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			}
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_recognition_progress value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.recognition_goal_gain compare = less_than }
		}
		AND = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_logistics_goal
			SOV = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_vulnerability value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.league_threat_gate compare = greater_than }
			}
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_depot_control value = constant:soviet_collapse_regional_faction.depot_gain compare = less_than }
		}
	}
}

is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = {
	OR = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_baltic_league_member
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_caucasus_league_member
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_central_asian_league_member
	}
}

can_soviet_collapse_call_regional_league_defensive_war = {
	is_soviet_collapse_regional_faction_member = yes
	SOV = {
		exists = yes
		is_soviet_collapse_active = yes
		OR = {
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_progressive_release.severe_threat compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.severe_republic_pressure compare = greater_than_or_equals }
			check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_league_cohesion value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.league_threat_gate compare = greater_than }
		}
	}
	OR = {
		has_war_with = SOV
		can_declare_war_on = SOV
	}
}

can_target_soviet_collapse_breakaway_for_moscow_union_treaty = {
	tag = SOV
	FROM = {
		exists = yes
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
		is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
		NOT = { tag = SOV }
		NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
		NOT = { is_subject = yes }
		NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_republic_protected_from_external_dependency = yes }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_independence_resilience value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.target_resilience_ceiling compare = less_than }
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_influence_patronage_risk value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.target_patronage_ceiling compare = less_than }
	}
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.union_treaty_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.union_treaty_authority_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
}

can_target_soviet_collapse_breakaway_for_moscow_federal_compact = {
	can_target_soviet_collapse_breakaway_for_moscow_union_treaty = yes
	is_soviet_collapse_moscow_dominant_influence_for_from = yes
	FROM = {
		has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_moscow_union_treaty_offered
		is_soviet_collapse_republic_weak_for_external_pressure = yes
	}
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.federal_compact_threat_ceiling compare = less_than }
	check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_moscow_authority value = constant:soviet_collapse_moscow_reintegration.federal_compact_authority_floor compare = greater_than_or_equals }
}

can_target_soviet_collapse_breakaway_for_foreign_protection_treaty = {
	FROM = {
		exists = yes
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_breakaway
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_event_created_republic
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_high_chaos_successor
			has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target
		}
		is_soviet_collapse_breakaway_country = yes
		NOT = { tag = ROOT }
		NOT = { tag = SOV }
		NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
			NOT = { is_subject = yes }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_dependency_recent }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_protection_treaty_signed }
			NOT = { is_soviet_collapse_republic_protected_from_external_dependency = yes }
		is_soviet_collapse_republic_weak_for_external_pressure = yes
		has_soviet_collapse_dynamic_foreign_dependency_resilience_room = yes
	}
	is_soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_candidate = yes
	is_soviet_collapse_client_patron_style = yes
	OR = {
		FROM = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_patron_selected_target }
		has_soviet_collapse_foreign_aid_route_to_from = yes
	}
	SOV = { is_soviet_collapse_foreign_intervention_pressure_open = yes }
	NOT = { has_country_flag = soviet_collapse_foreign_dependency_sponsor_recent }
	has_soviet_collapse_target_acceptance_for_foreign_aid_from_root = yes
	is_soviet_collapse_root_dominant_sponsor_for_from = yes
	has_soviet_collapse_dynamic_foreign_dependency_influence_ready_for_from = yes
}

	OR = {
		has_war_with = SOV
		check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_recognition_progress value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.large_recognition_gain compare = greater_than }
		SOV = {
			OR = {
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_total_collapse_threat value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.league_threat_gate compare = greater_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.league_threat_gate compare = greater_than }
			}
		}
	}
}

				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_military_obedience value = constant:soviet_collapse_soviet_objective.contested_obedience compare = less_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_foreign_appetite value = constant:soviet_collapse_release_gate.foreign_pressure compare = greater_than_or_equals }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_republic_confidence value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_pressure_high compare = greater_than }
				check_variable = { var = soviet_collapse_old_movement_pressure value = constant:soviet_collapse_republic_focus.ai_old_movement_pressure_high compare = greater_than }
			}
		}

	}
